Die »Furor«, sagte Sánchez am Rande der Generalversammlung der Vereinten Nationen in New York, sei »mit allen Mitteln« ausgestattet, um die Aktivisten zu retten, falls das nötig würde. Man werde das Recht spanischer Staatsbürger verteidigen, sicher durchs <a href="https://archive.ph/o/NmtPe/https://www.spiegel.de/thema/mittelmeer/" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-weight:400;border-bottom-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;cursor:pointer;display:inline;text-decoration-color:rgb(0, 0, 0);text-decoration-line:none;text-decoration-style:solid;text-decoration-thickness:auto;">Mittelmeer</a> zu navigieren. (<em style="font-style:italic;border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;">Mehr über die Ausrüstung der begleitenden Kriegsschiffe <a href="https://archive.ph/o/NmtPe/https://www.spiegel.de/ausland/gaza-krieg-was-kann-die-flottillen-eskorte-a-8bd990f0-a4b5-4a62-abb2-aa21d17a1ce4" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-weight:400;border-bottom-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;cursor:pointer;display:inline;text-decoration-color:rgb(0, 0, 0);text-decoration-line:none;text-decoration-style:solid;text-decoration-thickness:auto;">lesen Sie hier</a>.</em>)</div>

Die letzte Etappe der Vuelta a España, eines der wichtigsten Radrennen der Welt, musste abgebrochen werden, weil 100.000 propalästinensische Demonstranten die Strecke stürmten.                                                                         <h3 style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-family:SpiegelSansUI, system-ui, BlinkMacSystemFont, -apple-system, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Oxygen, Ubuntu, Cantarell, &quot;Fira Sans&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:24px;font-weight:700;border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;margin-block-end:32px;margin-block-start:48px;margin-bottom:32px;margin-inline-end:0px;margin-inline-start:0px;margin-left:0px;margin-right:0px;margin-top:48px;">»Wir wissen, wie man den Terrorismus besiegen kann«</h3>
                                                                        <div style="font-size:20px;border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;line-height:1.5;margin-block-end:24px;margin-block-start:0px;margin-bottom:24px;margin-inline-end:0px;margin-inline-start:0px;margin-left:0px;margin-right:0px;margin-top:0px;"><span style="border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden;width:33.333333333333336%;"></span>Die Frage, woher diese enge Verbindung rührt, wird besonders gern diskutiert, wenn die deutsche und die spanische Sichtweise auf den Konflikt aufeinandertreffen.</div>
                                                                        <div style="font-size:20px;border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;line-height:1.5;margin-block-end:24px;margin-block-start:0px;margin-bottom:24px;margin-inline-end:0px;margin-inline-start:0px;margin-left:0px;margin-right:0px;margin-top:0px;"><span style="border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden;width:33.333333333333336%;"></span>Und so stand Sánchez jüngst beim Antrittsbesuch des Kanzlers neben <a href="https://archive.ph/o/NmtPe/https://www.spiegel.de/thema/friedrich_merz/" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-weight:400;border-bottom-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;cursor:pointer;display:inline;text-decoration-color:rgb(0, 0, 0);text-decoration-line:none;text-decoration-style:solid;text-decoration-thickness:auto;">Friedrich Merz</a> und versuchte sich an einer Antwort. Nun ja, sagte Sánchez, Spanien sei ein mediterranes Land. Um die Stabilität im Mittelmeerraum sorge man sich nicht nur aus humanitären Gründen – sondern auch aus geopolitischen.</div>
                                                                    </div>
                                                                </div>
                                                                <div style="border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;">
                                                                    <div style="border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;"></div>
                                                                </div>
                                                                <div style="border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;">
                                                                    <div style="font-family:SpiegelSerifUI, Constantia, &quot;Lucida Bright&quot;, Lucidabright, &quot;Lucida Serif&quot;, Lucida, &quot;DejaVu Serif&quot;, &quot;Bitstream Vera Serif&quot;, &quot;Liberation Serif&quot;, Georgia, serif;border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;overflow-wrap:break-word;padding-left:24px;padding-right:24px;width:66.66666666666667%;">
                                                                        <div style="font-size:20px;border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;line-height:1.5;margin-block-end:24px;margin-block-start:0px;margin-bottom:24px;margin-inline-end:0px;margin-inline-start:0px;margin-left:0px;margin-right:0px;margin-top:0px;"><span style="border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden;width:33.333333333333336%;"></span>Außerdem, so Sánchez, habe die spanische Gesellschaft selbst Erfahrung mit blutigen Attentaten gemacht. Die baskische Terrorgruppe Eta legte die Waffen am Ende freiwillig nieder, nach langen Verhandlungen. »Wir wissen, wie man den Terrorismus besiegen kann. Und er wird sicherlich nicht so besiegt, wie es Israel, wie es die Regierung Netanyahu tut«, sagte Sánchez. »Man kann ihn nicht besiegen, indem man einen wahllosen Angriff auf die Zivilbevölkerung durchführt, der mehr als 60.000 Menschen das Leben kostet.«</div>
                                                                    </div>
                                                                </div>
                                                                <div style="border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;">

                                                                        <div style="font-size:20px;border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;line-height:1.5;margin-block-end:24px;margin-block-start:0px;margin-bottom:24px;margin-inline-end:0px;margin-inline-start:0px;margin-left:0px;margin-right:0px;margin-top:0px;"><span style="border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden;width:33.333333333333336%;"></span>Was Sánchez beim Treffen mit Merz unterschlug, ist die historische Dimension der Verbindung mit den Palästinensern. Schon zu Zeiten der Diktatur pflegte Spanien gute Beziehungen zu den arabischen Staaten. Diktator Francisco Franco nutzte sie, um sich aus der internationalen Isolation zu lösen. In den Jahren der Transition setzte sich das fort. Adolfo Suárez, erster Regierungschef der Demokratie, empfing Palästinenserführer <a href="https://archive.ph/o/NmtPe/https://www.spiegel.de/thema/jassir_arafat/" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-weight:400;border-bottom-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;cursor:pointer;display:inline;text-decoration-color:rgb(0, 0, 0);text-decoration-line:none;text-decoration-style:solid;text-decoration-thickness:auto;">Jassir Arafat</a> in Madrid mit einer Umarmung – obwohl der <a href="https://archive.ph/o/NmtPe/https://www.spiegel.de/thema/plo/" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-weight:400;border-bottom-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;cursor:pointer;display:inline;text-decoration-color:rgb(0, 0, 0);text-decoration-line:none;text-decoration-style:solid;text-decoration-thickness:auto;">PLO</a>-Führer damals im Westen als Paria galt.</div>
                                                                    </div>

                                                                        <div style="font-size:20px;border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;line-height:1.5;margin-block-end:24px;margin-block-start:0px;margin-bottom:24px;margin-inline-end:0px;margin-inline-start:0px;margin-left:0px;margin-right:0px;margin-top:0px;"><span style="border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden;width:33.333333333333336%;"></span>Den Staat Israel erkannte Spanien erst 1986 an, um der Europäischen Gemeinschaft beitreten zu können. Anschließend trat man als Vermittler auf, setzte sich für eine Zweistaatenlösung ein. 1991 fand im Königspalast von Madrid eine Friedenskonferenz statt.</div>

                                                                        <div style="font-size:20px;border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;line-height:1.5;margin-block-end:24px;margin-block-start:0px;margin-bottom:24px;margin-inline-end:0px;margin-inline-start:0px;margin-left:0px;margin-right:0px;margin-top:0px;"><span style="border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden;width:33.333333333333336%;"></span>Für die spanische Linke ist die palästinensische Sache seit Jahrzehnten identitätsstiftend. Sie wird verstanden als antikoloniale Bewegung, ähnlich wie die der <a href="https://archive.ph/o/NmtPe/https://www.spiegel.de/ausland/westsahara-sie-wollen-ihre-heimat-zurueck-oder-alle-auf-demselben-friedhof-liegen-a-3274d7fe-b73b-4577-bbe4-c459c6499886" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-weight:400;border-bottom-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;cursor:pointer;display:inline;text-decoration-color:rgb(0, 0, 0);text-decoration-line:none;text-decoration-style:solid;text-decoration-thickness:auto;">Sahrawis</a>, die in der <a href="https://archive.ph/o/NmtPe/https://www.spiegel.de/thema/westsahara/" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-weight:400;border-bottom-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;cursor:pointer;display:inline;text-decoration-color:rgb(0, 0, 0);text-decoration-line:none;text-decoration-style:solid;text-decoration-thickness:auto;">Westsahara</a>, einer ehemaligen spanischen Kolonie, für einen eigenen Staat kämpfen.</div>
                                                                        <div style="font-size:20px;border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;line-height:1.5;margin-block-end:24px;margin-block-start:0px;margin-bottom:24px;margin-inline-end:0px;margin-inline-start:0px;margin-left:0px;margin-right:0px;margin-top:0px;"><span style="border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden;width:33.333333333333336%;"></span>Doch auch Teile der Rechten, beeinflusst von der katholischen Kirche, sehen den israelischen Umgang mit Christen in der Region kritisch. »Die Identifikation mit den Glaubensbrüdern im Nahen Osten hat spürbaren Einfluss«, sagt der Historiker Alejandro Salamanca. Israelkritik sei in Spanien kein rein linkes Phänomen. Selbst unter rechten Wählern spricht eine Mehrheit vom »Genozid« in Gaza.</div>

                                                                    <div style="font-family:SpiegelSerifUI, Constantia, &quot;Lucida Bright&quot;, Lucidabright, &quot;Lucida Serif&quot;, Lucida, &quot;DejaVu Serif&quot;, &quot;Bitstream Vera Serif&quot;, &quot;Liberation Serif&quot;, Georgia, serif;border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;overflow-wrap:break-word;padding-left:24px;padding-right:24px;width:66.66666666666667%;">
                                                                        <h3 style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-family:SpiegelSansUI, system-ui, BlinkMacSystemFont, -apple-system, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Oxygen, Ubuntu, Cantarell, &quot;Fira Sans&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:24px;font-weight:700;border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;margin-block-end:32px;margin-block-start:48px;margin-bottom:32px;margin-inline-end:0px;margin-inline-start:0px;margin-left:0px;margin-right:0px;margin-top:48px;">Waffenembargo gegen Israel</h3>
                                                                        <div style="font-size:20px;border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;line-height:1.5;margin-block-end:24px;margin-block-start:0px;margin-bottom:24px;margin-inline-end:0px;margin-inline-start:0px;margin-left:0px;margin-right:0px;margin-top:0px;"><span style="border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden;width:33.333333333333336%;"></span>Instinktpolitiker Sánchez hat diese Spaltung der Rechten längst erkannt – und nutzt sie, um von Korruptionsvorwürfen gegen seine Partei abzulenken. Seit Monaten sucht Sánchez gezielt den öffentlichen Streit mit der Regierung von <a href="https://archive.ph/o/NmtPe/https://www.spiegel.de/thema/benjamin_netanyahu/" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-weight:400;border-bottom-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;cursor:pointer;display:inline;text-decoration-color:rgb(0, 0, 0);text-decoration-line:none;text-decoration-style:solid;text-decoration-thickness:auto;">Benjamin Netanyahu</a>.</div>
                                                                        <div style="font-size:20px;border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;line-height:1.5;margin-block-end:24px;margin-block-start:0px;margin-bottom:24px;margin-inline-end:0px;margin-inline-start:0px;margin-left:0px;margin-right:0px;margin-top:0px;"><span style="border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden;width:33.333333333333336%;"></span>Bereits im vergangenen Jahr erkannte die spanische Regierung <a href="https://archive.ph/o/NmtPe/https://www.spiegel.de/thema/palaestina/" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-weight:400;border-bottom-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;cursor:pointer;display:inline;text-decoration-color:rgb(0, 0, 0);text-decoration-line:none;text-decoration-style:solid;text-decoration-thickness:auto;">Palästina</a> als Staat an – gemeinsam mit <a href="https://archive.ph/o/NmtPe/https://www.spiegel.de/thema/irland/" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-weight:400;border-bottom-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;cursor:pointer;display:inline;text-decoration-color:rgb(0, 0, 0);text-decoration-line:none;text-decoration-style:solid;text-decoration-thickness:auto;">Irland</a>, <a href="https://archive.ph/o/NmtPe/https://www.spiegel.de/thema/norwegen/" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-weight:400;border-bottom-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;cursor:pointer;display:inline;text-decoration-color:rgb(0, 0, 0);text-decoration-line:none;text-decoration-style:solid;text-decoration-thickness:auto;">Norwegen</a> und <a href="https://archive.ph/o/NmtPe/https://www.spiegel.de/thema/slowenien/" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-weight:400;border-bottom-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;cursor:pointer;display:inline;text-decoration-color:rgb(0, 0, 0);text-decoration-line:none;text-decoration-style:solid;text-decoration-thickness:auto;">Slowenien</a>. Damals schüttelten in <a href="https://archive.ph/o/NmtPe/https://www.spiegel.de/thema/europa/" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-weight:400;border-bottom-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;cursor:pointer;display:inline;text-decoration-color:rgb(0, 0, 0);text-decoration-line:none;text-decoration-style:solid;text-decoration-thickness:auto;">Europa</a> noch viele den Kopf, nun sind Länder wie <a href="https://archive.ph/o/NmtPe/https://www.spiegel.de/thema/frankreich/" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-weight:400;border-bottom-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;cursor:pointer;display:inline;text-decoration-color:rgb(0, 0, 0);text-decoration-line:none;text-decoration-style:solid;text-decoration-thickness:auto;">Frankreich</a> und <a href="https://archive.ph/o/NmtPe/https://www.spiegel.de/thema/grossbritannien/" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-weight:400;border-bottom-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;cursor:pointer;display:inline;text-decoration-color:rgb(0, 0, 0);text-decoration-line:none;text-decoration-style:solid;text-decoration-thickness:auto;">Großbritannien</a> auf Sánchez-Linie.</div>
                                                                        <div style="font-size:20px;border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;line-height:1.5;margin-block-end:24px;margin-block-start:0px;margin-bottom:24px;margin-inline-end:0px;margin-inline-start:0px;margin-left:0px;margin-right:0px;margin-top:0px;"><span style="border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden;width:33.333333333333336%;"></span>Doch der Ministerpräsident geht längst weiter. Sánchez wirft Israel »Völkermord« und die »Ausrottung eines wehrlosen Volkes« vor. Er<a href="https://archive.ph/o/NmtPe/https://www.spiegel.de/kultur/musik/esc-auch-spanien-droht-mit-boykott-bei-teilnahme-israels-a-52b201f2-9046-488a-8624-4159cf803212" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-weight:400;border-bottom-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;cursor:pointer;display:inline;text-decoration-color:rgb(0, 0, 0);text-decoration-line:none;text-decoration-style:solid;text-decoration-thickness:auto;"> droht mit einem Boykott des </a><a href="https://archive.ph/o/NmtPe/https://www.spiegel.de/thema/eurovision_song_contest/" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(0, 0, 0);font-weight:400;border-bottom-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(92, 90, 88);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;cursor:pointer;display:inline;text-decoration-color:rgb(0, 0, 0);text-decoration-line:none;text-decoration-style:solid;text-decoration-thickness:auto;">Eurovision Song Contest</a>, falls Tel Aviv teilnehmen darf. Sánchez fordert zudem den Ausschluss des Landes von internationalen Wettkämpfen. In dieser Woche verkündete er schließlich ein vollständiges Waffenembargo, selbst »dual use«-Güter, die für zivile und militärische Zwecke genutzt werden können, dürfen nun nicht mehr geliefert werden.</div>
                                                                    </div>
                                                                </div>
                                                                <div style="border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;">
                                                                    <div style="border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;"></div>

Die beiden linken Ministerinnen Sira Rego und Yolanda Díaz dürfen nicht mehr nach Israel einreisen. Vizeregierungschefin Díaz reagierte unversöhnlich: »Dass ein Staat, der Völkermord begeht«, ihr die Einreise verwehre, empfinde sie als Ehre.</div>

                                                                        <div style="font-size:20px;border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:inline;line-height:1.5;margin-block-end:0px;margin-block-start:0px;margin-bottom:0px;margin-inline-end:0px;margin-inline-start:0px;margin-left:0px;margin-right:0px;margin-top:0px;"><span style="border-bottom-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:0px;border-image-outset:0;border-image-repeat:stretch;border-image-slice:100%;border-image-source:none;border-image-width:1;border-left-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-right-style:solid;border-right-width:0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 219, 217);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:block;overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden;width:33.333333333333336%;"></span>In den nächsten Tagen könnte Sánchez’ Eskalationsstrategie auf einen neuen Höhepunkt zulaufen. Am Wochenende soll die »Furor« die 53 Aktivistenschiffe erreichen, die zurzeit in der Nähe Kretas Schutz vor schlechtem Wetter suchen. Sobald sie weitersegeln, könnte es zum Showdown kommen – auch wenn das Verteidigungsministerium Berichten zufolge ihre Beamten angewiesen hat, sich den Aktivisten nicht zu sehr zu nähern. Doch selbst die Bilder einer spektakulären Rettungsaktion, wie Sánchez sie in New York in Aussicht gestellt hat, würden im spanischen TV rauf und runter laufen. Von den Korruptionsskandalen der Sozialisten spräche dann erst mal niemand mehr.</div>
